---
title     : "TypedBarendregt: Raw terms with types (broken)"
layout    : page
permalink : /TypedBarendregt
---

This version uses raw terms. Substitution presumes that no
generation of fresh names is required.

The substitution algorithm is based on one by McBride.
It is given a map from names to terms. Say the mapping of a
name is trivial if it takes a name to a term consisting of
just the variable with that name. No fresh names are required
if the mapping on each variable is either trivial or to a
closed term. However, the proof of correctness currently
contains a hole, and may be difficult to repair.

## Values do not reduce

Values do not reduce.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Val-⟶"></a><a id="12950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12956" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12958" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12960" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12961" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12963" class="Bound">N</a><a id="12964" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12966" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9195" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="12974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12961" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12976" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12978" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="12980" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12981" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12961" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9462" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="12985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12963" class="Bound">N</a><a id="12986" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9345" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="12998" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="13001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9223" class="InductiveConstructor">Zero</a> <a id="13012" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="13015" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13021" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9268" class="InductiveConstructor">Suc</a> <a id="13026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13026" class="Bound">VM</a><a id="13028" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13030" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9777" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="13037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13037" class="Bound">M⟶N</a><a id="13040" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="13043" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="13046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13026" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="13055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13037" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As a corollary, terms that reduce are not values.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⟶-Val"></a><a id="13134" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13134" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="13140" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13142" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13144" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13145" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13147" class="Bound">N</a><a id="13148" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13150" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13152" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13145" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9462" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="13157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13147" class="Bound">N</a><a id="13158" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13160" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13162" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="13164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9195" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="13170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13145" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="13172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13134" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="13178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13178" class="Bound">M⟶N</a> <a id="13182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13182" class="Bound">VM</a>  <a id="13186" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="13189" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13182" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="13198" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13178" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Reduction is deterministic

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="det"></a><a id="13258" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13258" class="Function">det</a> <a id="13262" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13264" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13266" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13267" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13269" class="Bound">M′</a> <a id="13272" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13272" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="13274" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="13278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13280" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13267" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9462" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="13285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13269" class="Bound">M′</a><a id="13287" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="13306" class="Comment">----------</a>

<a id="14780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13258" class="Function">det</a> <a id="14784" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#10538" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="14789" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="14793" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#10538" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="14800" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="14804" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14806" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14808" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Almost half the lines in the above proof are redundant, for example

    det (ξ-·₁ L⟶L′) (ξ-·₂ VL _) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L′)
    det (ξ-·₂ VL _) (ξ-·₁ L⟶L″) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L″)
 
are essentially identical. What we might like to do is delete the
redundant lines and add

    det M⟶M′ M⟶M″ = sym (det M⟶M″ M⟶M′)

to the bottom of the proof. But this does not work. The termination
checker complains, because the arguments have merely switched order
and neither is smaller.

## Canonical forms

## Progress

## Preservation

### Domain of an environment

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17892" class="Comment">{-
dom : Ctx → List Id
dom ε            =  []
dom (Γ , x `: A)  =  x ∷ dom Γ

dom-lemma : ∀ {Γ y B} → Γ ∋ y `: B → y ∈ dom Γ
dom-lemma Z           =  here
dom-lemma (S x≢y ⊢y)  =  there (dom-lemma ⊢y)

free-lemma : ∀ {Γ M A} → Γ ⊢ M `: A → free M ⊆ dom Γ
free-lemma (Ax ⊢x) w∈ with w∈
...                      | here         =  dom-lemma ⊢x
...                      | there ()   
free-lemma {Γ} (⊢λ {N = N} ⊢N)          =  ∷-to-\\ (free-lemma ⊢N)
free-lemma (⊢L · ⊢M) w∈ with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...                        | inj₁ ∈L    = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...                        | inj₂ ∈M    = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
free-lemma ⊢zero ()
free-lemma (⊢suc ⊢M) w∈                 = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢pred ⊢M) w∈                = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢if0 ⊢L ⊢M ⊢N) w∈
        with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...         | inj₁ ∈L                   = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...         | inj₂ ∈MN with ++-to-⊎ ∈MN
...                       | inj₁ ∈M     = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
...                       | inj₂ ∈N     = free-lemma ⊢N ∈N
free-lemma (⊢Y ⊢M) w∈                   = free-lemma ⊢M w∈       
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Substitution preserves types

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21722" class="Comment">{-
⊢subst : ∀ {Γ Δ ρ}
  → (∀ {x A} → Δ ∋ x `: A  →  Γ ∋ x `: A)
  → (∀ {x A} → Γ ∋ x `: A  →  Δ ⊢ ρ x `: A)
    --------------------------------------------------------------
  → (∀ {M A} → (⊢M : Γ ⊢ M `: A) →  ok ⊢M  →  Δ ⊢ subst ρ M `: A)
-}</a>
<a id="⊢subst"></a><a id="21966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21966" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="21973" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21975" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21977" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21978" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="21980" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21980" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="21982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21982" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="21983" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="23065" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="23068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#2881" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢if0</a> <a id="23073" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21966" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23042" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23051" class="Bound">⊢L</a><a id="23086" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23088" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23089" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21966" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23096" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23042" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23054" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23101" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23103" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21966" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23042" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23057" class="Bound">⊢N</a><a id="23116" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="23118" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21966" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23125" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23125" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23128" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="23132" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23132" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23134" class="Symbol">)</a>                <a id="23151" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="23154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="23157" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21966" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23165" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23125" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23132" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23170" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let's look at examples.  Assume `M` is closed.  Example 1.

    subst (tm-∅ , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x")  ≡  `λ "y" `→ M

Example 2.

      subst (tm-∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ subst (tm-∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M , "y" ↦ ` "y") (` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ (M · ` "y")

The hypotheses of the theorem appear to be violated. Drat!
